Scott High School">Layman E. Scott High School</a>. Various churches and private foundations operate several private schools.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Colleges_and_universities">Colleges and universities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Colleges and universities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:St_Matthews_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/St_Matthews_2.jpg/220px-St_Matthews_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="143" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/St_Matthews_2.jpg/330px-St_Matthews_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/St_Matthews_2.jpg/440px-St_Matthews_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="444" data-file-height="289" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:St_Matthews_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/St._Matthew%27s_University" title="St. Matthew&#39;s University">St. Matthew's University</a> campus</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/University_College_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="University College of the Cayman Islands">University College of the Cayman Islands</a> has campuses on Grand Cayman and Cayman Brac and is the only government-run university on the Cayman Islands.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> A hall at the University College of the Cayman Islands is named after Sir Vassel Johnson, who The Cayman Islands Financial Services Association credited as one of the founding fathers of the financial services sector in the Cayman Islands. Sir Vassel is also the only person to ever be knighted in any British Dependent Territory. <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.gov.ky/portal/page/portal/cighome/pressroom/archive/200811/governorstributetosirvassel">http://www.gov.ky/portal/page/portal/cighome/pressroom/archive/200811/governorstributetosirvassel</a>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/International_College_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="International College of the Cayman Islands">International College of the Cayman Islands</a> is a private college in Grand Cayman. The college was established in 1970 and offers associate's, bachelor's and master's degree programmes.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> Grand Cayman is also home to <a href="/wiki/St._Matthew%27s_University" title="St. Matthew&#39;s University">St. Matthew's University</a>, which includes a <a href="/wiki/Medical_school" title="Medical school">medical school</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Veterinary_school" class="mw-redirect" title="Veterinary school">school of veterinary medicine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_Law_School" title="Cayman Islands Law School">Cayman Islands Law School</a>, a branch of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Liverpool" title="University of Liverpool">University of Liverpool</a>, is based on Grand Cayman.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/The_Cayman_Islands_Civil_Service_College" title="The Cayman Islands Civil Service College">The Cayman Islands Civil Service College</a>, a unit of Cayman Islands government organised under the Portfolio of the Civil Service, is in Grand Cayman. Co-situated with University College of the Cayman Islands, it offers both degree programs and continuing education units of various sorts. The college opened in 2007 and is also used as a government research centre.
</p><p>There is a <a href="/wiki/University_of_the_West_Indies" title="University of the West Indies">University of the West Indies</a> Open campus in the territory.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Health_and_emergency_services">Health and emergency services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Health and emergency services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>See <a href="/wiki/Health_in_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Health in the Cayman Islands">Health in the Cayman Islands</a>.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Emergency_services">Emergency services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Emergency services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Cayman_Islands_Police_Service" title="Royal Cayman Islands Police Service">Royal Cayman Islands Police Service</a> (RCIPS) provides law enforcement for the three islands. Regular off-shore <a href="/wiki/Marine_(ocean)" class="mw-redirect" title="Marine (ocean)">marine</a> and air patrols are conducted by the RCIP using a small fleet of vessels and a helicopter. Grand Cayman is a <a href="/wiki/Port#port_of_call" title="Port">port of call</a> for <a href="/wiki/UK" class="mw-redirect" title="UK">Britain's</a> <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">United States Coast Guard</a> who often assist with sea rescues when their resources are in the Cayman Islands area. The Cayman Islands Fire Service provides fire prevention, fire fighting and rescue.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Its headquarters are in George Town and has substations in Frank Sound, West Bay, Cayman Brac and Little Cayman.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg/220px-Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg/330px-Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg/440px-Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg 2x" data-file-width="639" data-file-height="639" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Grand_Cayman_Island.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Grand Cayman Island, from space</div></div></div>
<p>Access to Emergency Services is available using 9-1-1, the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_telephone_number" title="Emergency telephone number">Emergency telephone number</a>, the same number as is used in <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> and the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> The Cayman Islands Department of Public Safety's Communications Centre processes 9-1-1 and non-emergency law enforcement, EMS, fire, and <a href="/wiki/Search_and_rescue" title="Search and rescue">search and rescue</a> calls for all three islands. The Communications Centre dispatches RCIP and EMS units directly, however, the Cayman Islands Fire Service maintains their own dispatch room at the airport fire station.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Truman_Bodden_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Truman Bodden Stadium">Truman Bodden Sports Complex</a> is a multi-use complex in George Town. The complex is separated into an outdoor, six-lane 25-metre (82&#160;ft) swimming pool, full purpose track and field and basketball/netball courts. The field surrounded by the track is used for <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a> matches as well as other field sports. The track stadium holds 3,000 people.
</p><p>Association football is the national and most popular sport, with the <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_national_football_team" title="Cayman Islands national football team">Cayman Islands national football team</a> representing the Cayman Islands in <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2009)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>The Cayman Islands Basketball Federation joined the international basketball governing body <a href="/wiki/FIBA" title="FIBA">FIBA</a> in 1976.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> The country's <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_national_basketball_team" title="Cayman Islands national basketball team">national team</a> attended the official 2011 <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Basketball_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="Caribbean Basketball Championship">Caribbean Basketball Championship</a> for the first time.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Rugby_Union_in_the_Cayman_Islands" class="mw-redirect" title="Rugby Union in the Cayman Islands">Rugby union</a> is a developing sport, and has its own <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_national_rugby_union_team" title="Cayman Islands national rugby union team">national men's team</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_women%27s_national_rugby_union_team" title="Cayman Islands women&#39;s national rugby union team">women's team</a>, and Sevens team. The Cayman Men's Rugby 7s team is second in the region after the 2011 NACRA 7s Championship.
</p><p>The Cayman Islands is a member of <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>, the <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Pan_American_Sports_Organisation" class="mw-redirect" title="Pan American Sports Organisation">Pan American Sports Organisation</a>, and also competes in the biennial <a href="/wiki/Island_Games" title="Island Games">Island Games</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Cayman Islands is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Cricket_Council" title="International Cricket Council">International Cricket Council</a> which they joined in 1997 as an Affiliate, before coming an Associate member in 2002. The <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_national_cricket_team" title="Cayman Islands national cricket team">Cayman Islands national cricket team</a> represents the islands in <a href="/wiki/International_cricket" title="International cricket">international cricket</a>. The team has previously played the sport at <a href="/wiki/First-class_cricket" title="First-class cricket">first-class</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_A_cricket" title="List A cricket">List A</a> and <a href="/wiki/Twenty20_cricket" class="mw-redirect" title="Twenty20 cricket">Twenty20</a> level. It competes in <a href="/wiki/2012_ICC_World_Cricket_League_Division_Five" title="2012 ICC World Cricket League Division Five">Division Five</a> of the <a href="/wiki/World_Cricket_League" title="World Cricket League">World Cricket League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ICCP_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ICCP-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Squash is popular in the Cayman Islands with a vibrant community of mostly ex-pats playing out of the 7 court South Sound Squash Club. In addition, the women's professional squash association hosts one of their major events each year in an all glass court being set up in Camana Bay. In December 2012, the former Cayman Open will be replaced by the Women's World Championships, the largest tournament in the world. The top Cayman men's player, Cameron Stafford is No. 2 in the Caribbean and ranked top 200 on the men's professional circuit.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Flag_football" title="Flag football">Flag football</a> (CIFFA) has men's, women's and co-ed leagues.
</p><p>Other organised sports leagues include softball, beach volleyball, <a href="/wiki/Gaelic_football" title="Gaelic football">Gaelic football</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ultimate_frisbee" class="mw-redirect" title="Ultimate frisbee">ultimate frisbee</a>.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands_Olympic_Committee" title="Cayman Islands Olympic Committee">Cayman Islands Olympic Committee</a> was founded in 1973 and was recognised by the IOC (<a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a>) in 1976.
</p><p>In the 21st century, skateboarding has become popular among the youth.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In February 2010, the first purpose built track for <a href="/wiki/Kart_racing" title="Kart racing">kart racing</a> in the Cayman Islands was opened.<sup id="cite_ref-Compass_Track_Opening_100-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Compass_Track_Opening-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> Corporate karting Leagues at the track have involved widespread participation with 20 local companies and 227 drivers taking part in the 2010 Summer Corporate Karting League.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music">Music</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Music">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Music_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Music of the Cayman Islands">Music of the Cayman Islands</a></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Cayman_National_Cultural_Foundation" title="Cayman National Cultural Foundation">Cayman National Cultural Foundation</a> manages the F.J. Harquail Cultural Centre and the US$4&#160;million Harquail Theatre. The Cayman National Cultural Foundation, established in 1984, helps to preserve and promote Cayman folk music, including the organisation of festivals such as Cayman Islands International Storytelling Festival, the Cayman JazzFest, Seafarers Festival and Cayfest.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Jazz" title="Jazz">jazz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Calypso_music" title="Calypso music">calypso</a> and <a href="/wiki/Reggae_music" class="mw-redirect" title="Reggae music">reggae</a> genres of music styles feature prominently in Cayman music as celebrated cultural influences.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> Many of Cayman-inspired pop songs belong to these forms of music styles.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>There is one print newspaper currently in circulation throughout the islands: the <i>Cayman Compass</i>. There are numerous online news services including Cayman News Service and the Cayman Compass online edition. A local television station, CITN – Cayman 27, shows Cayman Islands news.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/List_of_radio_stations_in_Cayman_Islands" class="mw-redirect" title="List of radio stations in Cayman Islands">Local radio stations</a> are broadcast throughout the islands.
</p><p>Feature films that have been filmed in the Cayman Islands include: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Firm_(1993_film)" title="The Firm (1993 film)">The Firm</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Haven_(film)" title="Haven (film)">Haven</a></i>, <i>Cayman Went</i><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> and <i>Zombie Driftwood</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_Caymanians">Notable Caymanians</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Notable Caymanians">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<p><b><a href="/wiki/Geographic_coordinate_system" title="Geographic coordinate system">Lat. and Long.</a> <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion"><a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=Cayman_Islands&amp;params=19_20_N_81_24_W_"><span class="geo-default"><span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location"><span class="latitude">19°20′N</span> <span class="longitude">81°24′W</span></span></span><span class="geo-multi-punct">&#xfeff; / &#xfeff;</span><span class="geo-nondefault"><span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">19.333°N 81.400°W</span><span style="display:none">&#xfeff; / <span class="geo">19.333; -81.400</span></span></span></a></span> (George Town)</b>
